The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of  Sri Lanka
IMPORTANT  NOTICE  REGARDING  ACCEPTANCE  OF  NOTICES
FOR  PUBLICATION  IN  THE  WEEKLY  “GAZETTE”
ATTENTION is drawn to the Notification appearing in the 1st week of every month, regarding the latest dates and times of accept ance
of Notices for publication in the weekly Gazettes, at the end of every weekly Gazette of Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazettes  shall close at 12.00 noon of each Friday, two weeks before the date of
publication. All Government Departments, Corporations, Boards, etc. are hereby advised that Notifications fixing closing dates and times
of applications in respect of Post-vacancies, Examinations, Tender Notices and dates and times of Auction Sales, etc. should be  prepared
by giving adequate time both from the date of despatch of notices to Govt. Press and from the date of publication, thereby enab ling those
interested in the contents of such notices to actively and positively participate please note that inquiries and complaints mad e in respect
of corrections pertaining to notification will not be entertained after three months  from the date of publication.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazette should reach Government Press two weeks before the date of publication i.e.
Notices for publication in the weekly Gazette of 21st November, 2014 should reach Government Press on or before 12.00 noon on  07th
November, 2014.
Electronic Transactions Act, No. 19 of 2006 - Section 9
“Where any Act or Enactment provides that any proclamation, rule, regulation, order, by-law, notification or other matter shall
be published in the Gazette, then such requirement shall be deemed to have been satisfied if such rule, regulation, order, by-l aw,
notification or other matter is published in an electronic form of the Gazette.”.
P. H. L. V . D
E SIL V A,
 Acting Government Printer.
Department of Govt. Printing,
Colombo 08,
January 01, 2014.
This Gazette can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk

Service Conditions :
1. The posts are permanent and pensionable.
2. The appointment will be subject to a probation period of
3 years.
3. In addition to these recruitment and regulations, the
appointees will be subject to Establishment Code, Financial
Regulations, Departmental Orders and Regulations and
Orders which will be enacted from time to time by the
Government or Southern provincial Council.
General Conditions of Recrutiment :
01. Applicant should be a citizen of Sri Lanka by decent or
registration.
02. Applicant should have moral character and be in good
health.
03. Applicant should prove their permanent residence for the
period of recent three years within the area of Sooriyawewa
Pradeshiya Sabha.
04. Age should not be less than 18 years and not more than 45
years as at the closing date of applications. But age limit is
not applicable for those who are already employed in
Public Service or Provincial Public Service.
05. Qualified persons will be selected through written/
structural/practical interview as necessary.
06. Applicant should not have been convicted or punished by
a Court of Law under Penal Code or dispelled from Public
Service or Provincial Public Serivce.
07. Full powers of delaying or changing or amending this
recruitment after or in between calling application are
reserved with the Chairman of Sooriyawewa Pradeshiya
Sabha.
08. Priority will be given to those who have service experience.
Method of application .– Applicants should apply through an
application prepared as per the specimen given at the end of this
notice on or before 25.11.2014 to "Chairman, Pradeshiya Sabha,
Sooriyawewa under registered post. On the top left hand corner of
the envelope post applied for has to be mentioned. Late applications
will be rejected.
Photocopies of following certificates should be attached to the
application :
1. Certificate of Birth,
2. Educational Certificates,
3. Certificate of proving residence (counter signed by
Divisional Secretary),
4. Two recent testimonials,
5. Certificates of other qualifications or service experience,
6. A copy of the certificate of proficiency relevant to the
post.
Incomplete applications will be rejected and only applicants who
have possessed basic qualification will be called for the interview.
J. E
RANDA JANAKA,
Chairman,
Sooriyawewa Pradeshiya Sabha.
14th October, 2014.

02. Technical skills required - recruitment for the service category
of Semi Technical Grade III :
* Electrician :
(i) Should have obtained a certificate of proficiency at the
level of N. V . Q.-4 issued by a technical/vocational
training institute recognized by Tertiary Education
Commission pertaining to the furnctions of the post.
(ii) Should have obtained 03 year experience at the relevant
field in a recognized institute (Should confim by a
certificate of service).
Technical skills required - recruitment for the service category of
Technical Grade III :
* Driver :
(i) Should have obtained certificate of proficiency (Driving
License Grade A) issued by the Commissioner of Motor
Traffic for dirivng motor vehicles more than 34 Hundreds
in weight and buses capable of carrying passengers more
than 32.
(ii) Should have 03 years experience as a vehicle driver.
(Should have a certificate of service).
* Heavy Vehicle Operator :
(i) Should have obtained certificate of proficiency (Driving
License Grade A) issued by the Commissioner of Motor
Traffic for dirivng motor vehicles more than 34 Hundreds
in weight and buses capable of carrying passengers more
than 32.
(ii) Should have 03 years experience as a heavy vehicle
operator. (Should have a certificate of service).
03. Other Qualification required :
(i) The applicant should be a citizen of Sri Lanka.
(ii) Should not be less than 18 years or more than 45 years of
age on the date of closure of applications.
(iii) The applicant should be a permanent resident within the
administrative limits of Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala not
less than a period of 3 years on the date of closure of
application. (residence should be confirmed by electroal
register or certificate issued by the Divisional Secretary).
(iv) Should have an excellent character and should be in good
health.
(v) Should not have been convinced guilty of an offense by a
Court of Law under the Penal Code.
(vi) Male appilcants only should apply for the post of driver.
04. Method of recruitment.– Qualified candidates will be recruited
for these posts through an interview and oral/practical and
theorectical test according to the post.
05. Terms of employment :
(i) This post is permanent and pensionable.
(ii) This appointment will be subject to a probations period
of 3 years.
(iii) In addition to these recruitmetn conditions, applicant
should be abide by the conditions set out in the
Establishment Code, Financial Regulations, conditions
and regulations issued by the North Western Provincial
Public Service Commission and provisions set out in
Ordinances/Acts of Local Government Authorities and
orders issued by the Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala.
06. Method of application :
(i) Application prepared in accordance with the specimen
application given in this notification should be sent by
registered post to "Secretary, Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala,
Pannala" on or before 15.11.2014.
(ii) The post applied for should be indicated at the top left
hand corner of the envelope in which application is enclosed
as application for the post of "..............".
(iii) Photo copies of following certificates should be annexed
to the application :
* Certificate of Birth,
* Certificate of Education,
* School leaving certificate,
* A copy of National Identity Card,
* Certificate of Grama Niladhari for confirmation of
residency (certified by the Divisional Secretary),
* Two character certificates recently obtained,
* Certificate of experience.
The Secretary of the Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala reserves the
absolute authority to delay this recruitment or cancel or amend this
notification after of while applications are invited.
M. P. C. R
ENUKA,
Secretary,
Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala.
Pradeshiya Sabha Pannala,
14th October, 2014.

10–963
KALUTARA  URBAN   COUNCIL
Imposing Assessment Tax for the Year 2015
IT is hereby notified that the following resolution was taken in the
General Meeting held on 02nd day of September 2014 under the
decision No. 6:1:2.
It is further notified that the Assessment Tax imposed for the
year 2015 should be paid to the Urban Council in four euqal
installments within every quarter. If the assessment tax is for the
year 2015 paid in full before 31st of January 2015, a discount of ten
percent (10%) will be paid from the relevant assessment tax. When
assessment tax is paid in quarterly, if the tax is paid before the final
date of the first month of the quarter, a dsicount of five percent (5%)
will be paid from the relevant assessment tax.
Deshakeerthi Al-Haj M. M. M. J
AVUFER,
The Mayor,
Kalutara Urban Council.
On this day of 22nd September, 2014.

JA-ELA  URBAN  COUNCIL
Ordinance Property Rates for - 2015
IT is hereby notified tha tthe Urban Council Ja-Ela has in term of the
section 160(3) of the Urban Council's Ordinance (Chapter 255)
imposed the following rates for the year 2015 within the
administrative limits of Ja-Ela town.
(a) A rate of twelve per centum (12%) per annum on the
annual value of all commercial premises ;
and
(b) A rate of three per centum (3%) per annum on the annual
value of all other immovable properties.
Situated within the administrative limits of Ja-ela town payable
in four equal installments on or before March 31st, June 30th,
September 30th and December 31st respectively.
M. S
HAMMIKA DIAS,
Chairman,
Urban Council Ja-ela.
Urban Council Ja-Ela,
16th October, 2014.

IN terms of section No. 7(2) Butchers Ordinance (Chapter 272) it is
hereby notified that the person referred to in the following schedule

and that if any person residing within the limits of Wattala-Mabole

WARIYAPOLA    PRADESHIYA   SABHA
Business Tax for the Year 2015
HEREBY, the general pubilc in informed that the Pradeshiya Sabha of Wariyapola has adapted has decision No. III at the general meeting
held on 14th August, 2014.
The Pradeshiya Sabha further informes that these busineses tax should be paid before 30th April of each year.
ANANDA JAYALATH,
Chairman,
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola.
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola,
19th September, 2014.
THE PROPOSAL (DECISION)
A business which is required to obtain a permit from Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola as per the conditions stipulated in sentence
(1) of the Pradeshiya Sahba Act, No. 150 of 1987 or as per the conditions stipulated in any by-law has developed based an the p aid Act
or an enterprise listed in the attached list and in not required to pay a tax and an activity which is not a vocation, was in e xistence within
the boundaries of the Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola in year 2015, that business shall pay a business tax out of the income of th e year
2014, if the business takes within the subject numbers listed in column I of the attachments II and according to the amounts sp ecified in
column II of the attachments.
(a) An entrepreneur whose enterprise was exiting on 31st December, 2014 shall pay said tax to the Pradeshiya Sabha,
Wariyapola before 30th April, 2015.
(b) A entrepreneur whose business commanded in 2015 shall pay the paid tax to the Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola within
a month from the decision commencement.

WARIYAPOLA  PRADESHIYA  SABHA
Imposing Assesment Tax for the Year 2015
IT is hereby notified that the following resolution was adopted
under Resolution No. V of Pradeshiya Sabha meeting held on 14th
August, 2014 by virtue of powers vested in Pradeshiya Sabha
Wariyapola under Section 1 of Section 134 of Pradeshiya Sabha
Act, No. 15 of 1987.
The tax for the Year 2015 should be paid to the Pradeshiya
Sabha in four equal instalments in each quarter before on 31st
March, 30th June, 30th September, 31st December.
A 10% discount is granted to the tax payer when the full amount
of tax is paid before 31st January, 2015. A 5% discount is granted
to the tax payer when the full amount of the quarter instalment is
paid before the last day of the first month of each quarter.
A
NANDA JAYALATH,
Chairman,
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola.
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola,
19th September, 2014.

properties located within Padeniya, Hanhamunuwa,

WARIYAPOLA   PRADESHIYA   SABHA
Imposing Acreage Tax for the Year 2015
IT is hereby notified that the following resolution was adopted
under Resolution No. VI of Pradeshiya Sabha meeting held on 14th
August, 2014 by virtue of powers vested in Pradeshiya Sabha
Wariyapola under Section 3 of Section 134 of Pradeshiya Sabha
Act, No. 15 of 1987.
It was further announced that the Acreage Tax for the Year 2015
should be paid in four equal installments within the quarters ending
on 31st March, 30th June, 30th September and 31st December,
2015.
A discount of 10% will be granted to tax payers who pay the
full amount of the annual value before end of January, 2015 and 5%
discount will be granted to individuals who pay the full amount of
the instalment of the quarter before the end of first month of the
each quarter.
Additional charge of 15% will be imposed when the tax payers
fail to pay the tax by the end of each quarter.
A
NANDA JAY ALATH,
Chairman,
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola.
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola,
19th September, 2014.

"The following tax are imposed on lands that are located within
the area under preview of Wariyapola Pradeshiya Sabha and not
exempted from Acreage Tax under the provision of Article 135 of
the Local Government Act, No. 15 of 1987 and either permanently
or regularly under cultivations the authority vested upon Wariyapola

a land of 05 or more Hectares for the Year 2015.

in the Section IV(a) of the Government Gazette dated
10.03.1989 as the area comes under purview of Wariyapola
Pradeshiya Sabha as a special area under the authority
vested upon the minister under the Article 134(3) of the
Local Government Act, No. 15 of 1987, the Pradeshiya
Sabha imposes an Annual Tax of Rs. 50 per 01 Hectare for
the lands more than 01 Hectare and less than 05 Hectares
that are located within the area under purview of
Wariyapola Pradeshiya Sabha ;
(c) It is hereby notified by the virtue of powers vested in
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola under Section 134(6) of
Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 that the above
mentioned tax should be paid to the Pradeshiya Sabha in
four equal instalments in each quarter before on 31st March,
30th June, 30th September, 31st December, 2015.".

WARIYAPOLA  PRADESHIYA  SABHA
A Tax on Undeveloped Lands
HEREBY the general public in informed that the Pradeshiya Sabha
of Wariyapola has proposed the proposal No. XIII at the general
meeting held on 14th August, 2014 the impose an annual tax based
on the asset vaule of an undeveloped land which in located within
the boundaries of the Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola.
A
NANDA JAY ALATH,
Chairman,
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola.
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola,
19th September, 2014.
PROPOSAL
A land located within the boundarium of the Pradeshiya Sabha,
Wariyapola that units for building construction or agricultural
purposes or when, according to the genuin openion of the Pradeshiya
Sabha, the land could be developed for such a purpose ; and
(a) When no buildings was constructed in the land ; or
(b) When, according to the norms the Pradeshiya Sabha,
proportion between the land floor area covered by the
buildings and total land area of the land is smaller than the
proportion between the actual floor area of buildings and
the total land areas of the land ; or
(c) When the land in not being properly cultivated the
Pradeshiya Sabha, Wariyapola shall impose an annual tax
equal to 1% of the asset value of the land on the owner of
the land an per the sentence 153(1) of the Act, No. 15 and
1987.

of 6th Sub-article of 134 in Pradeshiya Sabha Act.

annual tax totally, according to the Section 134(7) of this act follows :

year is paid before 31st January, 2015.

and it is paid during the first month of the quarter.

PROPOSAL

the sub article (1) of article 153 in Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of
1987.

and if,

3:2 from the whole land, it is less than the average of
whole land.
It is consider as undeveloped land and to charge above tax for
the year 2015, before 31st March, 2015.

PROPOSAL
According to the authority, given to the pradeshiya sabha under the sub article (1) of article 152 in Pradeshiya Sabha act No. 15
of 1987.
(a) Under the orders of this act, it is proposed to charge a business tax from each and every person doing a business in
Dickwella pradeshiya sabha area in year 2015 and when the business income of the previous year belongs to the limits
of the mentioned subjects in 1st column of the following sub list and the amounts of 2nd column.
(b) This tax should be paid to the pradeshiya sabha-Dickwella before 30th June of 2015 by any person subject to the tax
according to the authority of sub article (3).

BANDARAWELA   MUNICIPAL  COUNCIL
Taxes Impose for the Year 2015
THE Bandarawela Municipal Council has decided to impose a
assessment tax referring to chapter 252 Municipal Council Ordinance
of 1947 Act, No. 29 under section 230 (1) the following percentage
will be charged from the rate payers.
02. According to the Sub Schedule No. 03 the Bandarawela
Municipal Council has taken a decision that the land in the
Municipal Council limits should be temporary valued by the Revenue
Officers of the Council and according to the Sub schedule No. 04
the Assessment Tax will be imposed from 01.01.2015.
03. Further the taxes should be paid on or before quarterly
ending on the March 31st, June 30th, September 30th and December
31st.
04. If the taxes are paid by the rate payers on or before 31st of
January 2015 a 10% discount will be allowed. If the rate payers
pays there taxes on working days on or before 30th of the first
month of every quarter a 5% discount will be allowed.
05.  Failing to pay the rates in time according to the sub schedule
02, 15% of fine will be impost for residential houses and 20% of
fine will be imposed for bare lands, building under construction
hotels and guest houses.

URBAN  COUNCIL  - MINUWANGODA
Notification under Chapter 255 of the Urban Council Ordinance
I, K. Fedrick Alahakoon, Chairman of the Minuwangoda Urban Council hereby announced that a resolution numbered 4ix was moved by
me and the same was seconded by the Hon. U. B. Prematilaka, the Deputy Chairman of the same Council and passed unanimously at the
general meeting oof the Minuwangoda Urban Council held on 25.08.2014 in terms of power vested by the sub section A(1) of in section
165 of the Urban Council Ordinance (Chapter 255) to impose and recover a licensing charge from any license issued for the year 2015
related to all premises used for the purposes highlighted in the following first line with effect from 01.01.2015 as depicted i n the
proportion of rates specified in the said Schedule against each business or industry.
Further, it is also noticed that these license fees given in the under mentioned Schedule to be paid by 31st March 2015.
K. FEDRICK ALAHAKOON,
Chairman,
Minuwangoda Urban Council.
